@b{Der}

[220.lpp.]
@2{2 Von der Zukunfft vnd Menſchwerbung}
@v{Der Hymnus vnd Lobgeſang zum Advent;}
@l{Veni Redemtor gentium,}
I.
NVn nahtz tahß Paſẜaules Peſtitais/
Tahß Jumprawas Bährns attſihtz/
Par ko ẜöw brienoyahs wiſẜa Paſẜaule/
Deewam tada Peedſimbſchana pattiek.
2. Nhe no Wiera Aſẜini/ neds no Meeſẜu/
Bett ween no to Ꞩwähtu Gharru/
Girr Deewa Wahrds tappis Zillwähx/
Vnd ſeed weenas Ꞩeewas Auglis.
3. Tahß Jumprawas Meeſẜa apgrutenata tappa/
Tomähr pallicka Ghods ſkieſts pagglabbohts/
Attſpiedeya daſchadi krahßni Dahwani/
Deews by ẜawà Ghodibà.
4. Wings ißghaya aran ẜawu Kambari/
To ſkieſtu Koniņja Dſiewohkli/
Patteeß Deews vnd Zillwähx/
Ꞩawu Zeļļu tätzädams ſteids.
5. Wings ißtetzeya no Thäwu/
Vnd ghreeſehs attkal py Thäwu/
Brautze Elles dibbinà/
Vnd attkal py Deewa Krähßlu.
6. Katters tu eſẜi tam Thäwam lieds/
Vßwarri ẜawahß Meeſẜahs/
Ka taws muhſchiegs Deewiegs Spähx/
Eekſchan mums to wayu Meeſẜu vhßturr. 
7. Tawa Ꞩille ſpied ſpohſche vnd krahßne/
Tai Nacktei gir jauns Ghaiſchums/
Tumſibai nhe buhß nahkt eekſchan/ 
Ta Titziba palleek allaſch ſkaidra. 
8. Ghods gir Deewam tam Tähwam ẜatziet/
Gohds gir Deewam winja Dählam/
@b{Ghods}

[221.lpp.]
@3{JEſu Chriſti. 3}
Ghods gir Deewam tam Ꞩwähtam Gharram/
Allaſchien vnd muhſchiege/ Amen.
@v{Jm Thon: Vom Himmel hoch da}
@v{kom ich her/} @l{etc.}
I.
SLawähtz gir taß wiſẜewallditais Deews/
Katters par mums apſchäloyeehs gir/
Vnd ẜuhtiyis ẜawu wiſẜemiļaku Dählu/
No ẜöw dſimbtu auxtakà Ghodà.
2. Ka taß muhſẜo Peſtitays taptu/
Mums peſtitu no to Grähko Naßtu/
Vnd zaur ẜawu Schälaſtibu{Schlaſtibu} vnd Taißnibu/
Ewäßtu muhſchigà Skaidribbà.
3. O leela Schälaſtiba vnd Lehniba/
O dſiļļa Mieleſtiba!
Deews darra tahdu Darrbu/ ka tam nhe weens Zillwähx/
Neds Engelis par to ghanne patteikt warr.
4. Deews vßjämm muhſẜu Zillwäzigu Ghiemi/
Taß Radditaiß wiſẜo Leeto/
Wings nhe apſmey weenu nabbagu Ꞩeewu/
Ka tas Zillwähx taptu winjahß Meeſẜahß.
5. Ta Tähwa Wahrds no muhſchibas/
Tohp Meeſẜa wiſẜa Schkieſtiba/
Taß Eeẜakums vnde taß Ghalls/
Dodahß par mums leelohs Bähdohß. 
6. Kaß gir taß Zillwähx/ kaß gir winja Darrbs/
Ka Deews ẜawu Dälu par to dohd?
Kam mehß wayagham tai auxtakai Manntai/
Ka ta muhſẜo dehļ tha darra? 
7. Ock way teem Ļaudeem/ kattri töw nitzina/
To Schälaſtibu nhe ẜayäm/
Nhe gribb klauſẜiet{klaſẜiet} tha Dählu Balxnu/
Vs to palleek Deewa Dußmiba.
@b{8. O}

[222.lpp.]
@2{4 Von der Zukunfft vnd Menſchwerdung}
8. O Zillwähx/ ka tu to nhe proht
Tawam Koninjam prettie eedt/
Katters py töw nahk tick Lehnprahtiegs/
Vnd töwis tick ẜirrdige aißjämmahs. 
9. Ey vßjem to ſchodeen ar Preeku/ 
Ꞩataiſẜi tam to Zellu tawahß Ꞩirrds/ 
Ka taß warr nahkt tawà Prahtà/
Vnd tu dabbu no ẜawu Schälaſtibu. 
10. Padohd tam tawu Ꞩapraſſchanu/
Schini ſchelighà Attnahkſchanà/
Padohd wiņja Ꞩwähtibai
Tohs Darrbus tawas Taißnibas. 
11. Ja tu to darri/ tad buhß wings taws/
Paſẜargha töw par tahß Elles Mohkas/
Ja nhe/ tad töw labb ẜarghayeeß/
Aiſto wings töw aißſlähds tahs Debbeſẜes Durrwis. 
12. Ꞩawa pirrma Attnahkſchana ſchinni Paſẜaule/
Gir biyuſẜi lohte lehniga
Ta ohtra buhß ļohte barrga/
Teem Beßdeewigeem par leelu Mohku. 
13. Bett tee kattri eekſchan CHriſto ſtahw.
Ee=eeß tad leelà Preezibà/
Vnd buhß py to Engeļo Drauds/
Ka teem nheneekada Nhelaime wairs kaitehß. 
14. Tam Tähwam auxtà Ghodibà
Arr ẜawu weenu peedſimbtu Dählu/
Ta lieds arridſan tam Ꞩwähtam Gharram
Gir Gohds vnd Ꞩlawa muhſchiege/ Amen.

@l{Magnificat.}
Manna Dwehſẜele teitz to Kungu/ vnd mans Gharrs eepree-
zeenayahß par to Deewu mannu Peſtitayu.
Aiſto taß gir to Sämmoſchanu ẜawas Kallpones vß-
raudſiyis/ Redſi/ no ſcho laiku man ẜwähtu teix wiſẜii Bährno Bähr-
ni.
@b{Aiſto}

[223.lpp.]
@3{JEſu Chriſti. 5}
Aiſto taß gir leelu py mann darriyis/ katters ſpehtziegs gir/
vnd kattra Wahrds ẜwähtz gir.
Vnd winja Schälaſtiba palleek no weenas Zilltas ihs ohtras/
py teem/ kattri to biya.
Taß gir ſpehtziegs ar ẜawu Ällkonu/ vnnd ißkaiſẜa tohs kattri
ghräſni gir ẜawas Sirrds Prahta.
Taß gruhſch tohs Spehziegus no to Krähſlu/ vnnd pazeļļ
tohß Sämmoſchus aukſcham.
tohs Jßallkuſchu peepillda taß arr Labbibu/ vnnd attſtay tohs
Baggatus tuckſchus.
Taß peeminn tahß Schälaſtibas/ vnd vßpallieds ẜawam Kall-
pam Jſrael.
Ka taß gir runnayis muhſẜeem Tähweem Abraham/ vnd win-
ja Ꞩäklam muhſchiege.
Gohds gir tam Tähwam/ tam Dählam/ vnd tam Ꞩwähtam
Gharram/ Ka no pirrmo Eeẜakumu gir biyis/ vnd palleek muhſchie-
ge muhſcham/Amen.

Chriſtum muhſẜu Peſtitayu/ muhſchigu Deewu/ Marias
Dählu/ teitzam mehs muhſchiege/ Amen.

II.
@v{Von der Gebuhrt JEſu Chriſti.}
CHriſtum buhs mums ẜlaweht krahßne/
Tahß ſkieſtas Jumprawas Marias Dählu/
Tick tahl ka tha Myļa Ꞩaule ſpied/
Vnd ihs wiſẜas Paſẜaules ghallà ſtepyahs.
@b{2. Taß}

[227.lpp.]
@3{JEſu Chriſti. 9}
2. Taß ẜwähtz Radditais wiſẜas leetas
Apwilka Kalpa wahyu Meeſẜu/
Ka taß to Meeſẜu zaur to Meeſẜu attpeſtitu/
Vnd winja Raddiyums wißkim nhe taptu ẜamaitahtz.
3. Ta Deewa Schälaſtiba no auxtu Debbeſẜu/
Eeſchan tahs ſkieſtas Mahtes Meeſẜahs eedohdahs/
Weena Meitiņja näß weenu ſläppänu Naßtu/
Kattru ta Meeſẜa nhe paſinna.
4. Tas ghodiegs Nams tahs krahßnas Ꞩirrds/
Peepehſch Deewa Baſniza tohp/
Kattra nhe weenu Wieru aiſkarre neds adſinna/
No Deewa Wahrdu ta apgrutenata attraßta tappa.
5. Ta zeenigha Mahte gir to pedſimmuſẜi/
Kattru Gabriels papreekſche peeẜatziya/
Kattru ẜwähtz Janis ar Lehkſchanu paradiya/
Kad taß wehl ẜawas Mahtes Meeſẜahs ghulleya. 
6. Taß ghulleya Ꞩeena ļohte Nabbags/
To zeetu Ꞩilliet taß nhe apnicka/
Maß Peens wiņja Barriba by/
Katters nhe weenu Puttniņu ißalckt licka. 
7. Ta Debbeſẜa Draudſiba tadehl preezayahs/
Tee Engeļi dſeed{dſed} Deewam Ghodu/
Teem Nabbageem Ghanneem tohp ẜluddenahtz/
Taß Ghanns vnd Radditais wiſẜas Paſẜaules. 
8. Ꞩlawa/ Ghods vnd Patteitziba gir Thöw ſatzieta/
Chriſte/ peedſimbtz no ſkieſtas Jumprawas/
Arr Tähwu/ vnd to Ꞩwähtu Gharru/
No ſcho Laiku muhſchiege/ Amen.

@v{Gelobet ſeyſtu JEſu Chriſt.}
SLawähtz eſẜi tu JEſu CHriſt/
Ka tu Zillwähx peedſimmis eſẜi/
No weenas Jumprawas/ taß gir teeß/
Tapehtz preezayahs to Engeļo Draudſe/ @l{Kyrie eleiſon.}
@b{2. Tha}

[228.lpp.]
@2{10 Von der Gebuhrt}
2. Tha muhſchiege Thäwa weeniegs Bährns
Taggad eekſchan Ꞩilles tohp attraſts/
Eekſchan muhſẜu nabbagu Meeſẜu vnd Aſẜini
Aptehrpyahs tha muhſchiega Baggatiba/ @l{Kyrie eleiſon.}
3. Kattru wiſẜa Paſẜaule nhe apthwerr/
Taß ghull eekſchan Marias Klehpi/
Taß gir weens maß Bährnings tappis/
Katters wiſẜahs leetaß weens vßturr/ @l{Kyrie eleiſon/}
4. Taß muhſchiegs Ghaiſſchums eedt ſcheidt eekſchan/
Dohd tay Paſẜaaulei jaunu Spiedumu/
Taß ſpied labb widdu paſẜchà nacktiy/
Vnd mums par Ghaiſſchumas Bährnus darra/ @l{Kyrie eleyſon.}
5. Taß Dähls ta Tähwa ihſtäns Deews/
Weens Weeſẜis Paſẜaule tappa.
Vnd wedde mums no ſchahß Paſẜaules/
Vnd darrà mums parr Bährnus ẜawà Wallſtibà/ @l{Kyrie eleyſon.}
6. Taß gir wirrſẜon Semmes nahtzis nabbags
Ka taß par mums apſchälotohß
Vnd Debbeſẜys darritu baggatus/
Vnd ẜaweem myļeem Engeļeem liedſa/ @l{Kyrie eleiſon.} 
7. To gir taß wiß mums darriyis/
Ꞩawu leelu Mylaſtibu arr to parradiet/
Tadehļ preezayahß wiſẜa Chriſtita Draudſiba/
Vnd patteitz par to tam muhſchiege/ @l{Kyrie eleiſon.}
@l{Grates nunc omnes &c.}
LAideeta mums wiſẜeem patteickt/ Deewam muhſẜam Kun-
gham/ katters zaur ẜawu ẜwähtu Peedſimſchanu mums gir
attpeſtiyis no tha Wälla Spähku vnd Wallſtibu.
Tam peedärrahß/ ka mehs arr teem Engeļeem dſeedam/ alla-
ſchien Ghohds gir Deewam eekſchan Auxtibas.

@v{Vom Himmel hoch da kom ich her/}
NO auxtu Debbeſẜu es atteemu/
Es attnäſẜu jums labbu jaunu Wehſt/
@b{Ta-}

[229.lpp.]
@3{JEſu Chriſti. 11}
Taß labbahs Wehſtes es tick dauds attnäſẜu/
No teem es dſeedaht vnd runnaht gribbu.
2. Jums gir ſchodeen weens Bährnings peedſimmis/
No weenas ißrädſätas Jumprawas/
Weens Bährings tick ſkaiſts vnde krahßnis/
Tam buhß juhſẜo Preekam vnd jaukumam buht.
3. Taß gir taß Kungs Chriſtus muhſẜo Deews/
Taß gribb jums weſt no wiſẜu ļaun/
Taß gribb patz juhſẜo Peſtitais buht/
No wiſẜeem Ghräkeem dariet ſkieſtus.
4. Taß attnäß jums wiſẜu Schälaſtibu/
Kattru Deews taß Tähws gir ẜataiſẜiyis/
Ka jums arr mums Debbeſẜies/
Buhß dſiewoht nu vnd muhſchiege.
5. Tad jemmeta währa to ihſtänu Siem/
To Ꞩilli/ vnd ſkrandainus Autiņus/
Turr attrohdat juhs to Bährniņu/
Katters wiſẜu Paſẜaules vßturr vnd näß.
6. Tapehtz laideeta mums wiſẜeem preezateeß/
Vnd arr teem Ghanneem eeteekſchan/
Paluhkoht ko Deews mums gir ſkinkoyis/
Arr ẜawu myļu Dählu apghadayis.
7. Jemm währa manna Ꞩirds/ vnd paluhko/
Kaß ghull turr eekſchan Ꞩillites/
Kam peedärr taß krahßnis Bährnings/
Taß gir taß myļais JEſulins.
8. Ꞩummähtz atnahtz tu ghodiegs Weeſẜis/
To Grehzeneeku nhe eſẜi apſmadeyis/
Vnd nahtz py man eekſchan Waidu/
Ka buhß man töw par to patteikt?
9. O Kungs tu Radditayis wiſẜo leeto/
Ka eſẜi tu tappis tick ſemmiegs/
Ka tu teh ghulli ẜawituſcha Ꞩeena/
No kattru Lohps vnd Eſelis ähd.
@b{10. Vnd}

[230.lpp.]
@2{12 Von der Gebuhrt}
10. Vnd jebſch ta Paſẜaule buhtu daudskahrt tick platta/
No dahrgeems Ackmineems vnd Sältu darrita/
Tad buhtu ta töw tock dauds maſa/
Par weenu ſchauru Schupuliet.
11. Taß Blaweris/ vnd tahß Sieſchadrehbes/
Gir rupſch Ꞩeens vnd Lackatiņi/
Vß ko tu Konings tick leels vnd baggahts
Läppo/ iht buhtu tee tawa Däbbäſẜa Wallſtiba.
12. Taß gir töw ta nu pattitzis/
Ka tu man teeſcham{teeſchani} radietu/
Ka wiſẜahs Paſẜaules Spähx/ Ghods vnd Mannta/
Preekſchan töw nhe maxa/ nhe pallieds/ neds darra.
13. Ock mans wiſẜomiļais JEſulins/
Darees{Darrers} ẜöw ſkieſtu miextu Ghulltinyu/
Padduſẜehtees eekſchan mannas Ꞩirrds Wahzinyu/

14. No to es allaſch lyxmis äßmu/
Lähko vnd dſeedoh allaſchien/
To ihſtänu midſänamu Dſeeßmu/
Arr Ꞩirrds Preeku tick krahßne. 
15. Ghods vnd Ꞩlawa gir Deewam eekſchan auxtu Kräßlu/
Kaß mums eeſkinko ẜawu weenigu Dählu/
Par to preezayahs to Engeļo Draudſe/
Vnd dſeed mums tahdu jaunu Ghaddu/

@v{Vom Himmel kam der Engel Schaar.}
NO Däbbäſẜu nahtze to Engeļo Draudſe/
Paradiyahs teems Ghanneems ſkaidre/
Tee ẜatziya teems/ Weens kraßnis Bährnings/
Turr ghull eekſchan zeetu Ꞩill.
2. Eekſchan Bettlehem Davida Pilli/
Ka Micha to gir ſluddenayis/
Taß gir taß Kungs JEſus CHriſt/
Katters juhſẜo wiſẜo Peſtitais gir.
@b{3. Ta-}

[231.lpp.]
@3{JEſu Chriſti. 13}
3. Tapehtz buhß jums iht preezigeem buht/
Ka Deews ar jums gir ẜaliedſenayees/
Taß gir peedſimmis juhſẜo Meeß vnd Aſẜins/
Juhſẜo Brahlis gir ta muhſchiga Mannta.
4. Ko warr jums kaiteht Grähki vnd Nahwe/
Arr jums gir taß patteſẜe Deews/

Deewa Dähls gir tappis juhſẜo Draugs.

6. Pehtz Ghalla buhß jums tomehr ta Teeſẜa/
Juhs eſẜeta nu tappuſchi Deewa Raddi/
Tapehtz teitzeeta Deewam muhſchiege/
Pazeetige/ preezige allaſchien.

@v{Der Tag der iſt ſo frewdenreich.}
TA Deena gir no Preeku baggata/
Wiſẜai radditai leetai :/:
Aiſto Deewa Dähls no Däbbäſẜu=Wällſtibas
Par wiſẜu Zillwäka Prahtu
No weenas Jumprawas gir peedſimmis/
Maria tu eſẜi ißrädſäta/
Ka tu Mahte taptu:
Kaß noticka tick brieniſke?
Deewa Dähls no Däbbäſẜu=Wallſtibas
Taß gir Zillwähx{Zillwàhx} peedſimmis.
2. Weens Behrnings tick ẜlawäns
Gir mums ſchodeen pedſimis :/.
No weenas Jumprawas tick krahßnahs/
Par Preeku mums nabbageem Ļaudeem/
Ja nhe buhtu taß Behrnings mums peedſimmis/
@b{Tad}

[232.lpp.]

ſkannighu Balxni ļohte tee brehze/ Winja Attnahkſchana pamohde-
naya wiſẜu to Pili/ Darridams Deewiſkus Darrbus vnd Mahzibu.

wählähtz/ Wings wiſẜus Pretzeneekus vnd Naudu Maineneekus/
Arr Patagu ẜißdams ißdſinna.
5. Nhewäſẜälus taß wäſẜälus darriya/ Bährni to ghodeya/ taß
winja ſkaugheem ļohte ẜahpeya/ Ghribbädami teems by kluſẜu zeeſt/
Wings ẜatziya/ zittad brehx tee Ackminis.

@3{JEſu Chriſti. 37}

[264.lpp.]
@2{46 Von der Himmelfahrth}
Ꞩlahweyeeta to/ ẜlahweyeeta to/

Wälls/ Ghräki vnd tha muhſchiga Nahwe/

tra gir eekſchan Ghrähko Pammeſſchanu.

tahs Nahwehs/ vnd ißtaiſẜitu muhſẜas Kahyas vß tha Meera Zeļļu.

ſchohs/ AMEN.

@v{Am Tag der Heimſuchung Mariae.}

@v{Am Tage Michaelis.}

niſku Mais/ Vnd attpeſty mums arridſan no muhſẜeems ghruteems
Ghräkeems/ Tad ghribbam mehs arridſan labpraht peedohdt muh-
ẜeem Waideeneekeem.
4. Tam Wällam prettie ſtahw/ ka taß mums nhe peewiļļ/
Nhe kahdà Kahrdenaſchanà eewädd/ Neds py Jſẜamiſẜchana
ſpeeſch/ Bett mums no wiſẜu ļaun/ ſchehlige attpeßty.
5. Och myļais ſchehliegs Kungs/ ghauſẜini vnnd wayro 
mums ſchahdu tawu Dahwanu/ kattru mehs dabbuyuſchi äſẜam/ No
tawas leelas Lehnibas/ Eſẜi mums ſchehliegs allaſchien.
6. Aiſto O myļais Kungs/ Töw peedärr Ghohds vñ Teik-
ſchana/ Tawa gir ta Wallſtiba/ ta lieds arridſan ta Ghohdiba/ Ꞩla-
wähtz gir taws Wahrds/ muhſchige muhſcham/ Amen/

XVII.
@v{Von der heiligen Tauffe.}
@v{Chriſt vnſer HErr zum Jordan kam/} @l{etc.}
CHriſt muhſẜo Kungs py Jordans nahze/
Pehtz ẜawa Tähwa Prahtu :/:
@b{No}

[287.lpp.]
@3{Von der heiligen Tauffe. 69}
No to ẜwähtu Jahni to Chriſtibu jehme/
Ꞩawu Darrbu vnd Ammatu peepilldiet:
Tur gribbeya taß eeſtahdiet mums weenu Maſghaſchanu/
Vnd maſgaht mums no Ghräkeem/
Abẜliezenaht arridſan to ruhktu Nahwu/
Zaur ẜawu paſſchu{paſſch u} Aſẜini vnd Mohkahm/
Taß darriya mums weenu jaunu Dſiewoſchanu.
2. Tad klauſẜeeta vnd jemmeta wiſẜi währa/
Ko Deews patz dehwe to Chriſtibu :/:
Vnd ko ick kattram Chriſtitam titzeht buhß/
Ka taß warr atſtaht no willtigas Mahzibas/
Deews ẜacka/ vnd ghribb buhß Vhdenim buht/
Bett nhe ween tyhrs Vhdens/
Winja ẜwähtz Wahrds gir arridſan klaht/
Ar baggatu Gharru beß Mähru/
Taß gir ſcheit patz tas Chriſtitais.
3. To gir taß mums ſkaidre parradiyis/
Arr Siemehm vnd arr Wahrdeem :/:
Ta Tähwa Ballxnis tappa ſkannige/
Turr patt py Jordanes dſirrdähtz/
Wings ẜatziya/ taß gir mans myļais Dähls/
Py kattru man labbs prahtz gir/
To ghribbu es jums pawehleht/
Ka jums buhß to pareiſe klauſẜiet/
Vnd darriet pehtz winja Mahzibu.
4. Deewa Dähls arridſan patz ſcheit ſtahw/
Eekſchan ẜawas krahßnas Zillwähzibas :/:
Taß ẜwähtz Gharrs no Däbbäſẜu nahk/
Arr Balloſcha Ghimy apghehrbees/
Ka mums jo ſtippre titzeht buhß/
Kad mehs Chriſtiti tohpam/
Wiſẜa Triaidiba mums Chriſtiyuſẜi gir/
Arr to py mums wirſẜon Semmes/
Dſiewoht gir ẜadderreyuſẜees.
@b{Ꞩa-}

[288.lpp.]
@2{70 Von der heiligen Tauffe.}
5. Ꞩaweem Mahzekļeem pawehleya JEſus Chriſt/
Eita wiſẜà Paſẜauleh mahziet :/:
Ka ta eekſchan Ghräkeem paſuſta gir/
Vnd buhß no Ghräkeem attſtahtees/
Kaß titz/ vnd leekahß Chriſtitees/
Tam buhs zaur to ẜwähtam tapt/
Weens jauns Zillwähx taß dähwähtz tohp/
Katters muhſchige nhe war mirrth/
Tam buhß to Däbbäſẜo=Wallſtibu dabbuiht.
6. Kaß nhe titz tahdai leelai Schälaſtibai/
Taß palleek ẜawohs Ghräkohs :/:
Vnd gir paſuddenahtz tai muhſchigai Nahwei/
Dſiļļe Elles dibbinà/
Tam nhe pallieds nheneek ẜawa Ꞩwehtiba/
Wiß winja Darrbs gir paſuddis/
Tee eedſimbti Ghräki to ẜamaita/
Eekſchan kattreems taß gir peedſimmis/
Neds ſpeh ẜöw arridſan palliedſeht.
7. Ta Atz ween to Vhdeeni räds/
Ka Zillwäki Vhdeni ley :/:
Ta Titziba eekſchan Gharru to Spähku ẜaproht/
No JEſu Chriſti Aſẜini/
Vnd gir preekſchan to weena ẜarrkana Straume/
No Chriſti Aſẜini ẜarrkana darrita/
Kattra wiſẜu Wainu dſeedina/
Ko mehs no Adamu äſẜam dabbuyuſchi/
Vnd arridſan paſſchi darriyuſchi.

XVIII.
@v{Von der Chriſtlichen Buſſe.}
@v{Auß tieffer Noht ſchrey ich zu dir/} @l{etc.}
ARan dſiļeem Bähdeem eß peeẜautzu töw/
Kungs Deews paklauſẜi mannu Ꞩaukſchanu :/:
@b{Tawas}

[289.lpp.]
@3{Von der Buß. 71}
Tawas ſchähligas Auſẜis grees py mann/
Vnd vs mannu Luhkſchanu tahß attwerr/
Aiſto ja tu ghribbi to vßredſeht/
Kas Ghräki vnde nhepatteeß gir darrietz/
Kaß warr/ Kungs/ tad preekſchan töw pallickt?
2. Py töw nhe maxa nheneek ka Schählaſtiba ween/
Kad tu tohß Ghrähkus peedohd :/:
Taß gir tock wellte arr muhſẜu Darrbu/
Kad mehs wiß labbahke ghribbam dſiewoht/
Preekſchan töw nhe warr nhe weens leeliteeß/
Tapehtz buhß ick kattram preekſchan töw byteeß/
Vnd tawu{tawa} Schälaſtibu ghaidiet.     
3. Tapehtz gribbu eß vß Deewu zerreht/
Vß mannu Nopellnu nhe luhkoht :/:
Vß to mannai Ꞩirrdei buhß paļauteeß/
Vnd vß winja Lehnibu titzeht/
Kattru man ẜohla winja dahrgs Wahrds/
Taß gir mans Preex/ vnd ſtippra Pills/
To ghribbu es allaſchien ghaidiet.
4. Vnd jeb taß kaweyahß ihß paſſchu Nackti/
Vnd atkal ihß tam Rytam :/:
Tomehr buhß mannai Ꞩirrdei no Deewa Spähku/
Nhe iſẜamiſt neds bähdateeß/
Tha darra Jſrael ihſtäns Rads/
Katters no to Gharru raddietz gir/
Vnd ẜawu Deewu pagghaid.
5. Jeb py mums gir dauds Ghrähki/
Py Deewu gir wairahk Schälaſtibas :/:
Winja Rohka nhe mitt pallidſeht/
Zeek leela arridſan gir ta Waina/
Wings gir weens tas labbs Ghanns/
Kas Jſrael ißpeſtiet gribb/
No wiſẜeem ẜaweem Ghräkeem.
@b{Er-}

[290.lpp.]
@2{72 Von der Buß.}
@v{Erbarm dich mein O HErre GOtt/} @l{rc.} 
ABſchäloyeeß par man O Kungs Deews/
Pehtz tawas leelas Schälaſtibas :/:
Nomaſga/ darri ſchkieſtus mannus Noſegumus/
Eß atſiſtu mannus Ghräkus/ tee man ruhp/
Töw ween äßmu es ghräkoyis/
Taß gir prettieb mann allaſchien/
Taß{Tvß} ļauns preekſchan töw nhe warr paſtahweht/
Tu palleetz taißnis/ jeb tu ẜohdietz tohpi.
2. Raughi Kungs eekſchan Ghräkeem äßmu eß peedſimmis/
Eekſchan Ghräkeem manna Mahte mann ẜayehme :/:
To Taißnibu tu myļo/ vnd darri ſinnamu/
Tawas Ghuddribas apẜlähptu Paddomu/
Apẜlatzini mann Kungs arr Jſopo/

Balltahx nhe Ꞩneegs/ mannas Auſẜis tohp liexmas/
Wiſẜi manni Kauli eepreezenayahß/

Leetz nohſt no mann wiſẜu Nhetaißnibu :/:
Vnd darri ſchkieſt eekſchan mann to Ꞩirrdi/
Weenu jaunu Gharru eekſchan mann ghattawu darri/
Nhe mett mann nohſt no tawu Waigu/
Tawu ẜwähtu Gharru nhe jemm no mann/
To Preeku tawas Peſtiſchanas py mann attghrees/
Taß paprahtiegs Gharrs mann py töw vßturr.
4. Teem Beßdeewigeem ghribbu eß tawu Zeļļu/
Teems Ghräzeneekeems arridſan pamahziet/ :/:
Ka tee no ļaunu willtigu Zeļļu/
Zaur töw py töw attgreeſchahs/
Paſẜarrgi mann Kungs/ Deews mannas Peſtiſchanas/
Par to Ꞩohdu zaur Aſẜini eeſiemohtu/
Manna Mehle paẜluddena tawu jhſtänu Baußli/
Dohd ka manna Mutte tawu Ꞩlawu ißplatta/
@b{5. Nhe}

[291.lpp.]
@3{Von der Buß. 73}
5. Nhe weenu meeſẜigu Vpperi tu no mann praſẜi/
Es buhtu töw to arridſan dehwis/

@v{Derſelbige LI. Pſalm/ auff ein andere weiſe.}
@v{O HErre GOtt begnade mich/} @l{rc.}
O Kungs Deews abſchäloyeeß par mann/
Pehtz tawas Lehnibas eſẜi man ſchäliegs/
Dellde mannu Noſegumu/
Pehtz tawas leelas Schälaſtibas :/:
Vnd maſgha mann ſchkieſtu/ O Kungs Deews/
No wiſẜu mannu Noſegummu/

Katters eß eekſchan man attrohdu:
Vnd manni Ghräki gir allaſch preekſchan mann/

Vnd dehwi mann arridſan ſinnaht/
Tawu ghuddribu beß Bähdam/
Kattra gir apẜlähpta :/:

[292.lpp.]
@2{74 Von der Buß.}
Apẜlacki mann ar Jſopo krahßne/

Weenu ſchkieſtu Ꞩirrdi/ vß to eß zerru :/:
Weenu patteeſẜu Gharru darri jaunu eekſchan mann/
Nhe mett mann arridſan wiſkim no töw/

Dädſams=Vpperis wißnotaļļ/

Py kattras tu no Deewu tappi ẜuhtietz.
6. Vnd ka töw nheneeka peetruhktu/ Kad tu klauſẜiyi tawam
myļam Deewam/ Vnnd darriyi ko taß töw pawehleya/ By teem
Kraukleem Meeſẜas vnd Mais/ Töw allaſch peeneſt{peeneeſt} rytohs vnnd
wackarohs.
7. Kad tu ghulleyi appakſchan weenu Pa=Eggly/ Deewa
Engelis py töw nahze/ Attneſẜe töw ehſt vnnd dſerrt/ Tad ghayi tu 
gharru Zeļļu/ Lieds tam Kallnam Herobeam.
8. To Danieļu Deews arridſan nhe aißmirrſẜa/ Kad taß ſtar-
pan teem plehſẜigeem Swäreem ẜehdeya/ ẜawu Engeli peeẜuhtiya taß
tam/ Vnd licka tam Barribu peeneſt/ zaur ẜawu Kallpu Habacuc.
9. Joſephs eekſchan Egypteŗo Sem̃es pahrdohtz tappa/ No 
Warao to Koninju zeetumà kalltz/ Ꞩawas Deewabiyaſchanas dehl/
Deews zehle to par weenu leelu Kunghu/ Ka taß warreya ẜawu Täh-
wu vnd Braļus baŗŗoht.
10. Taß ſchehliegs Deews arridſan nhe attſtaya/ Tohß trieß
Wierus eekſchan karrſtu Vggunigu Zeppli/ Ꞩawu Engeli taß no-
ẜuhtiya/ Paſẜargaya tohß no Vgguns Lähßmeems/ Vnd palliedſe-
ya tohß aran wiſẜams Bähdahms.
11. Och Deews tu eſẜi taggad wehl tick baggahtz/ Ka tu eſẜi 
biyis muhſchige/ Manna Zerriba ſtahw wiſkim vs töw/ darri mann 
py mannas Dwehſẜeles baggatu/ Tad gir mann ghann ſcheitan vnd 
muhſchige.

XXIII.
@v{Vom Creutz/ Verfolgung vnd Anfechtung.}
@v{Was kan vns kommen an für Noht/} @l{etc.}
KAhda Waida warr mums notickt/ Kad mums taß Kungs patz
ghanna :/: Vnd meelo mums arr ẜawu Mais/ Vnd vs ẜawu
Ghannibu wadda: Ta lieds eepreezena muhſẜo Ꞩirrdi/ Vñ
dſirrdena arr to ẜalldu Vhdeni Ꞩawa zeenigha ẜwähta Gharra.
2. Ꞩawa dahrga Wahrda pehtz/ Taß mums wädd vs ihſtänu
Zeļļu :/: Nhe laiſch nhekahdà Laikà nhe eepreezatus/ Buhdahmus
Lixtà vnd Waidà: Tapehtz mehs allaſch drohſchi äſẜam/ Jrr paſſchà
Nahwes ähna vnd Mohkahm/ Aiſto tu Kungs eſẜi py mums.

zena vnd ẜunni :/: Tha Nelaime ẜlahpeena tahß Meeſẜas Karumu/
Ka ta nhe darra Bähdas/ Tam Gharram zaur to Ghräko Wainu/
kattra muhſẜà Mirrſtamà Meeſẜa gir/ Vnd allaſchien kuſtenayahß.

vßluhkoyam :/: Tawa ẜwähta Wahrda zeenigu Barribu/ Kattru
mehs muhſẜahs Ꞩirrdihß ghrämoyam: Kad mums taß Wälls arr
ẜawu Willtibu vßeedt/ Ta patti muhſẜu Dwehſẜel eepreezena/ Arr
tawu Gharra Pillnibu.
5. Tawa Lehniba vnd Schälaſtiba/ Tapehtz allaſch py mums
palleek :/: No ſcho Laiku vnd muhſchige/ Tu eſẜi muhſẜo Paghlabbo-

Wallſtibà/ Nammineeki vnd Ꞩaime.

muhſẜas Ꞩirrdes ẜattaiſẜa :/: Zaur ihſtänu Titzibu vnd Myläſtibu/

mums/ AMEN.

@v{Da es wol gieng/ mein Hertz vnd Sinn/} @l{etc.}

@b{py}

@3{vnd Anfechtung. 119}
py mann ſtahw/ Vnd pallieds to Naſtu panneſt/ Kad neds Laime/

2. Bett vs Deewu/ manna Ꞩirrds drohſche/ Allaſch preezige

breeßmigas bruņņas gir/ Wirſẜon Semmes nhe gir ohters tahds.

wahräti :/: Preekſchan mums kaŗŗo tas ihſtäns Wiers/ Kattru

@3{Von der Chriſtlichen Kirchen. 137}

vnd JEſu CHriſti Palligu vnd ſpähku/ Tee Paggaņi warr paſiet/

O Wiſẜewalldiegs Deews/ muhſchiegs Tähws/ weens
Konings tahß ghohdibas/ vnd Radditais Debbes
vnd Semmes/ zaur kattra Gharru wiſẜas leetas wall-
ditas/ zaur kattra ißredſeſchanu wiſẜas leetas ißttaiſẜietas
tohp/ katters tu eſẜi weens Deews tha Meera/ no kattru
wiſẜa Weenaidiba py mums nahk: Mehß luhdſam töw/
tu ghribbätu mums muhſẜus Ghräkus peedoht/ vnd ar
tawu Deewigu Meeru vnd Weenaidibu apdahwenaht/
ka mehß biedameeß vnd trieſẜädami tawam Wahrdam
kallpoyam/ vnd tu allaſchien no mums warrätu teicktz
tapt/ zaur JEſum CHriſtum/ @l{&c.}

tahß Myläſtibas/ kas töw atſieſt tas dſiewo/ kas

JEſum CHriſtum/ @l{&c.}

ẜarrgaſchanu preezigi vnd kluſẜi warram buht: Zaur

ſchan tawu Waighu.

vnd nhe ẜlepyam töw muhſẜus Noſegummus.

@v{Der erſte Pſalm.}
LAbb tam/ kas nhe ſtaigha eekſchan to Beßdeewiego Runnaß/
neds minn vs to Zeļļu to Ghrezeneeko/ neds ẜehſch kur tee
Mehditayi ẜehſch.
2. Bett gribbahs to Baußlu tha Kunga/ vnd runna no ẜawu
Baußlu deenas vnd nacktis.
3. Tas gir ka kahds kohx dehſtietz py teems Vhdens Vppeem/
katters ẜawus Augļus näß ẜawà laikà/ vnd winya Lappas nhe ẜa-
wieſt/ vnd ko darridams tas ißdohdas.
4. Bett tha nhe gir tee Beßdeewigi/ bett ka Pällus/ kattrus tas
Wehſch ißpuhſch.
5. Tapehtz nhe palleek tee Beßdeewigi Ꞩohdà/ neds tee Ghre-
zeneeki eekſchan to Taißno Pullku.
6. Aiſto taß Kungs paſieſt to zeļļu to Taißno/ bett to Beßdewi-
go zellſch ißniext.

@v{Der ander Pſalm.}
KApehtz tracko tee Paggani/ vnd tee Ļaudis runna tick wellte?

vs mann ẜatziyis gir/ Tu eſẜi mans Dähls/ ẜchodeen äßmu es töw
dſimmis.

@v{Der vierdte Pſalm.}

@v{Der 25. Pſalm.}
Weena Dſeeßma Dawida.
PEhtz töw Kungs illgoyas mann/ Mans Deews es zeŗŗu vs
töw/ Nhe laid mann kaunà tapt/ ka manni Eenaidneeki par
mann nhe preezayahs.
2. Aiſto nhe weens tohp kaunà kas töwis ghaida/ bett kaunà
buhs teem tapt/ tee nickni Neewatayi. (@l{vel} Nitzinatayi.)
3. Kungs rahdi man tawu zeļļu/ vnd mahzi man tawas Pähdas.
4. Waddi mann eekſchan tawas Teeſẜibas/ vnd mahzi mann/
Aiſto tu eſẜi tas Deews katters mann pallieds/ Jckdenas es töw
ghaidu.
5. Attmini Kungs tawas Schälaſtibas vnd tawas Lehnibas/
kattra no Paſẜaules Eeẜakummu biyuſẜi gir.
6. Nhe peeminn tohs ghräkus mannas Jaunibas vnd mannu
Pahrkahpſchanu/ Bett peeminn mannis pehtz tawas Schälaſtibas/
tawas lehnibas dehļ.
7. Tas Kungs gir labbs vnd rahms/ tapehtz pamahza tas tohs
Ghrehzeneekus vs to zeļļu.
